# Edge Program — Per-Story Prompts (standalone sessions)

**What this is:** one **`▶ Story prompt`** per *not-yet-completed* story across every epic, so any Trello card can be pulled and run in a fresh Claude Code session on its own (per the guide §0.4 convention). Companion to `edge_program_implementation_guide.md` (the stories' full tasks/AC live there) + `edge_program_technical_spec.md` (design) + `sport_data_platform.md`.
**Last updated:** 2026-06-18 _(refresh on any material change)_

🚨 **GLOBAL RUN-COMMAND CONVENTION (operator 2026-07-02 — applies to EVERY prompt/session, incl. mid-session):** whenever you tell the operator to RUN something, ALWAYS give (a) **WHERE — laptop or the EC2 box** (box commands must be the full `docker compose … exec … python scripts/X.py …` wrapper, `-e AWS_DEFAULT_REGION=us-east-2` for DuckDB-S3; see `services/dagster/aws/BOX_OPERATIONS.md`) and (b) the **FULL copy-pasteable command** (exact flags/paths/env — no prose "run the X script", no unfilled placeholders). The operator loses time chasing this otherwise.

**How to use:** copy a story's block into a fresh session. Blocks are **compact by design** — they inherit shared context by reference (§ = sections of the implementation guide). Every block assumes the **§0.1 conventions**: `dbtf` (not `dbt`); Snowflake via the Snowflake MCP, fully-qualified, no `USE`; never a live Snowflake query on a request path; `uv run python`; hand >1-min scripts to the operator; **do not git commit/push**; market-blind for non-market models (Principle 3); honest-framing for anything user-facing (no win-rate/edge claims). **CI gates BEFORE handoff (never hand off red code): Python → `uv run pytest` (Unit Tests CI); dbt → `dbtf build --select state:modified+` AND `dbtf compile` (both dbt-Build CI jobs) — all green first.** **Every session (model track included) ENDS with an `⏭️ Operator handoff`: the CI-gate result + run-order commands + a copy-pasteable `git add <paths>` of every changed/created file to commit (code, dbt, `sub_model_registry.yaml`, `ablation_results/*.md`, doc edits) + what NOT to commit (artifacts → S3/registry) — so the repo never drifts out of sync.**

**App stories — one fresh session per story:** run app work **one story at a time, each in its own clean session.** For any **[App]** story: open a fresh session, paste the **application-session bootstrap prompt** (persisted at **`app_session_bootstrap.md`**), then paste **exactly one** story block — build, then **end with the `⏭️ Operator handoff` checklist** (Lambda rebuild/deploy, dbt commands, scripts to run, the `git add` for files to deploy, changelog line, verify-after-deploy) so the operator knows exactly what to run. Do **not** chain multiple stories through one long-lived session. App surfaces marked **⏳ §0.3** are **not hand-authored here** — their prompt is *generated by the upstream model session as its final step* (§0.3), filled with the real served PG contract, then run as a normal (bootstrap + that block) app session.

> **🚨 APP TARGET (every `[App]`/`[App/serving]` block) — two live, one dead:** UI → **`frontend/` (Next.js) ONLY**; backend/API → **`app/backend/` (live FastAPI)**; ⛔ **legacy Streamlit UI (`app/streamlit_app.py`, `app/home.py`, `app/pages/`, `app/utils/`) — DO NOT EDIT.** Footgun: `app/` is half-alive (`app/backend/` is live; the rest is dead Streamlit), and Next.js has its own `frontend/app/`. First action in any app session: `cat frontend/package.json` to confirm Next.js; if doing UI work and you open `app/home.py` / `app/pages/*.py`, **STOP — wrong place.** (Full rule: guide §0.2.) A prior session edited the Streamlit UI by mistake (2026-06-18) — this guard prevents a repeat. **Changelog rule: any change the end user would notice ends with a `frontend/data/changelog.json` entry — under the MONDAY of the current week (weeks group Monday→Monday; append to that Monday's block, don't key by the literal ship date).**

**Status legend:** ⬜ open · 🔄 in progress · 🔒 gated · ✅ done (no prompt needed).

---

## 🐞 Open incidents — REGISTER + fix prompts (resolve before feature work)

> **🟥 ~~Railway MCP~~ — OBSOLETE (INC-16, 2026-06-27): we are OFF Railway entirely (plan CANCELLED).** Orchestration is **self-hosted Dagster OSS on AWS EC2** (`i-07594af1679f81c38`); deploys go through the **P5 CD** (merge to `main` → OIDC→SSM→`deploy.sh`) or **SSM Session Manager** for a box shell — NOT a Railway MCP/dashboard. Serving cache = **DynamoDB `credence-prod-serving-cache`** (no PG, no `DATABASE_URL`). Any "Railway / Railway-cron / Railway-PG" reference in older prompts is STALE.

> **🟥 DATA SOURCE = S3 LAKEHOUSE (DuckDB), NOT Snowflake — applies to EVERY pending story (hardened 2026-06-29).** The E11.1 program has migrated Snowflake → S3 parquet (W1–W6 done: `mart_pitch_*`, the odds/CLV/team/FanGraphs/posteriors/savant marts, `stg_batter_pitches`, … all now S3 parquet; **W7 drops the last Snowflake views + the feature/serving readers → end-state Cortex-ONLY**). **So any model/data/feature story reads from the S3 lakehouse via DuckDB — NOT Snowflake.** A Snowflake read is now a **RED FLAG** (the object is a thin external-table view today and GONE after W7); the only sanctioned Snowflake use is the Cortex narrative (`generate_pick_narratives.py`). Use the proven lakehouse-read pattern (DuckDB over S3 — `run_w1_lakehouse`/`zone_matchup` scripts); assemble the feature matrix ONCE→parquet for bake-offs (read the cache per candidate, never re-pull). If a source looks Snowflake-only, STOP + flag it as a likely un-migrated straggler (a precursor, not a Snowflake read). **Treat any "query Snowflake / `baseball_data.*` table" instruction in an OLDER prompt below as STALE → read the S3 parquet instead.**

A single contract's miss is NOT a null.

**E2.2 — ✅ GATE RAN 2026-06-22 — honest finding (NOT-MET = the finding, like E2.1b): home/away runs are essentially INDEPENDENT (residual ρ=−0.0035); the totals variance deficiency is MARGINAL UNDER-DISPERSION, not dependence.** Harness: `betting_ml/utils/copula.py` (discrete distributional-transform → normal-scores ρ estimator, `kendall_tau_to_rho`, vectorized `sample_gaussian_copula_negbin`, `analytic_total_variance`, `GaussianCopulaParams`) + `betting_ml/scripts/totals_generative/fit_copula.py` (OOS-purged-CV marginals, ρ + ρ/r bucket-conditioning, sim+analytic AC validation, **dispersion diagnostic**) + 14 tests `betting_ml/tests/test_copula.py`; `uv run pytest` 405✓/1s. **Operator run (11,659 eval games 2021–25):** residual ρ=−0.0035 (Kendall −0.0046, naive raw +0.0002) → **copula UNNECESSARY** (global, no material bucket ρ); corr AC ✅, but **var(total) AC ❌ — copula 15.15 ≈ independent 15.18 vs empirical 19.99 (~24% shortfall, identical with/without coupling)** ⇒ the gap is in the MARGINALS. **Root cause = under-dispersion: E2.1 fits NegBin `r` on optimistic TRAIN-fit means → `r` too high; the dispersion diagnostic confirms an OOS-calibrated `r` (~4 vs train ~6–15) reproduces var(total) → closes the gap.** **🔑 Load-bearing design choice (still correct):** ρ was fit on the RESIDUAL dependence after E2.1 conditional means absorb shared park/weather/ump (distributional-transform→normal-scores), NOT raw pairs (double-count). **➡️ E2.3 directives: (1) DROP the copula coupling (ρ≈0, convolve independently); (2) CALIBRATE the per-side dispersion on HELD-OUT residuals, not E2.1's train-fit r — that is the lever for calib_80≥0.80 / PIT.** Operator: re-run `fit_copula.py` once to bake the dispersion diagnostic into `ablation_results/e2_2_copula_fit.json` + `e2_2_copula_decision.md` (first run predated that block). `copula_v1.json` records ρ_global≈0.

🎯 LEAD WITH PITCHER STRIKEOUTS (operator synthesis 2026-06-24): of all props, `pitcher_strikeouts` is the strongest candidate market — a softer, lower-limit player-prop that books price off recent-start averages + pitcher reputation (Miller-Davidow's lazy non-featured pricing), and it plays directly to our EB/NegBin/Bayesian stack. It's a genuinely DIFFERENT market from the game-level ones we've exhausted (H2H dead ×5, main totals efficient, PA-vs-log5 null). ⚠️ Still a HYPOTHESIS held to E5.4's hard gate — we've found efficiency everywhere + props overfit easily — so realistic expectations + the trustworthy-null discipline apply.

DO — price each prop from the player's predictive distribution. **For pitcher_strikeouts specifically, model K = K-RATE × BATTERS-FACED**, each component explicitly:
 (1) **K-RATE** — NegBin/Poisson per-PA K rate with **EB CAREER + LEAGUE priors** (the small-sample shrinkage edge: early-season / post-return, shrink the raw rate toward career/league and let data take over as n grows). Condition on platoon split (vs LHB/RHB), pitch-arsenal composition, and ⭐ **CATCHER FRAMING** — the underweighted factor (borderline strike→K; we have the data, books rarely price it). **⚠️ TEMPER per E13.2 (2026-06-24): for PA outcomes, platoon/TTO added ≈0 CONDITIONAL on batter×pitcher identity (the signal is ~all identity, which log5 + any decent K model already capture). So do NOT lean the K edge on platoon/matchup conditioning — lean it on (a) the genuinely-underweighted CATCHER FRAMING, (b) the small-sample EB-shrinkage advantage early-season/post-return, and (c) the MARKET being lazy (the bet is the BOOK misprices K lines off recent-avg+reputation, NOT that we have a better matchup model). If the K-prop market turns out as efficient as the game-level ones, expect a clean null at E5.4 — and that's fine.**
 (2) **BATTERS-FACED — the K-opportunity DENOMINATOR via a SURVIVAL/hazard model of pitcher workload**: P(reach F5) / expected batters faced as a hazard on pitch-count + velocity-decay + run-environment + manager-pull tendency (we have the pitch-level velocity). This answers "how many ABs does this SP actually get," which the K count depends on.
 (3) **F5 SCOPING** — also price the FIRST-5-INNINGS K window (rides the E5.1 F5 backfill): removes bullpen noise, isolates the starter = the cleanest scope.
 Convolve (1)×(2) → the K-count predictive distribution → P(over/under) at the book's line. Also price the other phase-1 props (pitcher_outs from starter_ip_v1 directly; batter_total_bases/hits from the per-batter PA distribution), but pitcher_strikeouts is the LEAD.
Gate/AC: per-prop P(over/under) at the line; PIT-calibrated + per-prop reliability/ECE under E1.1 CV. ⇒ feeds E5.3 (edge/de-vig vs the K line) → **E5.4 (the HARD gate — the crux: calib_80, PBO<0.2/DSR>0 per market multiple-comparison-corrected, forward CLV NET OF the high prop vig)**. HONEST: calibration ≠ edge — a well-calibrated K distribution is product value (projections) even if E5.4 returns null. ⚠️ Needs the E5.1 K-prop backfill (in progress).

▶ Story prompt — E5.3 Edge, de-vig & per-book comparison — pitcher strikeout props   [Model-B · market-AWARE (de-vig); feeds E5.4]   (fleshed 2026-06-25)

🔑 THE E5.2-FLAGGED BLOCKER — NAME→ID BRIDGE: the E5.1 S3 K-prop lines key on `player_name` (NO player_id); the E5.2 predictions key on `pitcher_id`. **Wire the `ref_players` name→pitcher_id bridge to join them** — handle ambiguity (duplicate names, accents, Jr./Sr., nicknames). DO:
 • JOIN: load the E5.2 K predictive distribution per (pitcher_id, date) → join to the S3 K lines via the `ref_players` bridge → one row per (pitcher, date, book, K-line).
 • DE-VIG each book's two-way K price (over/under) → the book's de-vigged implied P(over) (reuse devig_*; two-sided at the line).
 • MODEL P at the book's EXACT line off the E5.2 distribution — P(K > line) for a half-line (e.g. 5.5), and handle the integer-line PUSH convention explicitly (e.g. line 6 → over = P(K≥7), push = P(K=6)); don't fudge the half vs integer.
 • EDGE = model P − book de-vigged P; EV per $1 at the book's offered price. Per book + a Pinnacle sharp-anchor column WHERE Pinnacle prices K props (⚠️ Pinnacle prop coverage may be thin → flag, don't assume).
 • OUTPUT: the per-(pitcher × date × book × line) prop edge/EV table + the join-coverage report → `ablation_results/e5_3_*` (and the shape E5.4 will read).
🔒 HONEST FRAMING (required): a transparency / model-vs-market comparison, NOT a bet rec. The prop VIG is LARGE → net-of-vig is the only honest read; "edge" here is model-relative and UNPROVEN until E5.4. No +EV claim.
Gate/AC: per-(pitcher×date×book×line) edge + EV table; per-book de-vig correct (two-way; integer-line push handled); name→id join-coverage report with unresolved flagged; Pinnacle anchor where available; honest framing; `uv run pytest -m "not slow"` green. Feeds E5.4.
Closeout (per §0.1): END with an ⏭️ Operator handoff — run-order + `git add` (the E5.3 module + table records + any ref-bridge code) + the join-coverage number + where the edge table lands.

```
▶ Story prompt — E5.4   ✅ **DONE 2026-06-29 — VERDICT = CLEAN NULL (committed + pushed to dev).** The K-prop edge thesis is CLOSED. Calibration floor MET (calib_80 0.8104 purged CV) but the edge gates FAIL: **PBO 0.421** (selection = noise), **DSR 0.246** (below chance after deflating 660 pre-registered configs), broad-strategy **ROI −3.14% net of vig over 44,851 bets** — negative EVERY season (2023 −5.8% → 2026 −3.6%) and EVERY book (−0.7% to −5.5%); the ~6.9% median prop hold eats the model's disagreement. The best in-sample config (+9.3%) placed ZERO out-of-sample bets (the data-mining trap, caught). Dossier `ablation_results/e5_4_prop_gate.{json,md}` + `e5_4_config_grid_results.csv` (all 660 logged); new `prop_gate.py` (20 tests); fast gate 810✅. ⚠️ caveat: the backtest is OPTIMISTIC (fit-on-tested-seasons) → a miss here is especially damning. ONLY-not-falsified = live forward CLV (needs a shadow harness + ≥100 forward live bets w/ +captured CLV net of vig to reopen) — prior is poor. **DOES NOT close the projection/transparency PRODUCT: the calibrated K distribution ships on E5.5 as honest projections + "where we differ from the book," NEVER a +EV rec.** (Orig prompt ↓.)   ⭐ ASSIGNED 2026-06-29 as the modeling-track slot.
🤝 **PARALLEL-SAFE — confirmed:** reads ONLY the cached `e5_3_prop_edge_table.parquet` + the E5.1 S3 closes (per §0.5) → **ZERO overlap with the live feature migration** (W8a/W8b touch `feature_pregame_*`; INC-22 touches the serving-write path; E5.4 touches NEITHER). No coordination needed; it's a self-contained offline gate.
🎯 **GOING-IN FINDING (honest expectation, NOT a license to skip the gate): E5.3 already showed the unbiased read is ≈ NULL** — two-sided `edge_over` ≈ 0 (mean −0.013), blind-over EV ≈ −8.7%/$1 net of vig. So a clean NULL is the LIKELY and fully-acceptable outcome. The value of this session = a DECISIVE, deflation-honest verdict that closes (or opens) the softest-market hypothesis — which tells you whether props warrant the E5.5 surface + live forward-capture build. Do NOT let the null expectation soften the discipline — the whole point is that the gate, not a hunch, decides; and equally, do NOT manufacture a pass (the §0.5 trap below).
WHY: E5.3 produces the per-book prop edge table; E5.4 DECIDES whether any of it is a REAL, cashable edge or a clean null. **This is THE gate** — props are the easiest place to overfit (many prop types × players × lines × books = a huge multiple-comparison surface), so the discipline here is non-negotiable. A calibrated K distribution (E5.2) is product value; whether it's PROFITABLE is decided ONLY here.
🔒 THE GATE (ALL required, ALL pre-registered BEFORE looking at outcomes):
 1. **CALIBRATION FLOOR** — calib_80 ≥ 0.80 per prop type under E1.1 purged walk-forward CV (E5.2 met this for K = 0.8104; re-confirm on the served glm + extend to any other prop type tested).
 2. **PBO < 0.2 AND DSR > 0 PER MARKET, multiple-comparison-corrected ACROSS EVERY prop-type × line × book tried** — DSR deflates for the number of configs, so **LOG EVERY combination tested** and feed the full count into the deflation. No cherry-picking the best-looking market.
 3. **POSITIVE FORWARD CLV NET OF THE (HIGH) PROP VIG vs the prop's OWN close** — the cashability gate. Offline edge is necessary-NOT-sufficient; the verdict is forward CLV on the actual prop closes, net of the large prop vig (gross "edge" that the vig eats is not edge).
 4. **COVERAGE/ROBUSTNESS report** — per-market sample sizes, edge distribution, sensitivity to the line/book set.
⚠️ THE TRAP (non-negotiable — the prop data-mining machine): "find the markets/lines where we'd have won" manufactures fake edges. The market/line/book SELECTION is PART of the test → pre-register the markets to test, select/fit IN-FOLD (never on the eval fold), count every config in the DSR deflation, judge on held-out/FORWARD CLV. A market that looks +EV in-sample but fails the deflated gate is REJECTED. (Same discipline as E13.9/E13.13.)
🔭 MEASUREMENT: forward CLV needs prop CLOSES going forward. E5.1 has the HISTORICAL closes (use them for the backtest leg); LIVE forward prop capture is an E5.0/E5.5-class enrichment not yet built → stand up forward accrual via the E13.5-style shadow harness, OR run the historical-close backtest now + flag that the FORWARD leg accrues live before any ship. Offline backtest = necessary; forward = the real verdict.
💾 DATA (per §0.5): reads the E5.3 edge table + the E5.1 S3 closes — S3/cached, NO fresh Snowflake pull.
Read: §5B E5.4 + §0 + §5 gates + E1.4 (the PBO/CSCV + DSR implementations) + E5.3 (the edge table this gates) + the E13.13 derivative-gate pattern (same forward-CLV-net-of-vig discipline) + `betting_ml` eval (purged CV / PBO / DSR / forward CLV).
DO: implement the gate over the E5.3 table; pre-register the prop markets/lines tested (write them down first); run purged-CV calib + PBO/DSR per market (multiple-comparison-corrected) + forward CLV net of vig vs the prop's own close; produce a clear SHIP/NULL verdict + a dossier (`ablation_results/e5_4_*`). IF a market clears → it's the program's FIRST real betting edge → flag for serving (the E5.5 prop app surface + the E10.2 uncertainty-aware sizing). IF null → dossier entry + close the K-prop hypothesis honestly.
HONEST EXPECTATION: **likely NULL** — H2H dead ×5, main total ~coinflip, E13.8 confirms market efficiency. A clean leak-tight null here is a PLAUSIBLE, ACCEPTABLE outcome (it completes the dossier + closes the K-prop hypothesis with integrity). A survivor = the FIRST real edge. **Do NOT let E5.2's "well-calibrated" get reframed as "profitable" — that's decided HERE, only.**

▶ Story prompt — E13.14 CROSS-MARKET RELATIVE-VALUE probe — internal consistency of the market constellation (the genuinely-untested mechanism)   [Model · 🧭 OPUS · ⭐ the NEW edge angle (operator 2026-06-30) · parallel-safe cached-odds eval · tests COHERENCE-BETWEEN-markets, NOT prediction accuracy]   (2026-06-30)
🟢 **READY-TO-RUN (PM 2026-07-19) — the TIER-2 lead edge probe (run after E2.1-r).** ⭐ Now the FRESHEST live edge candidate: the model-discrimination path (E1.11) and the line-timing path (E13.16) BOTH closed as trustworthy nulls (7/2, 7/5), so this market-NEUTRAL cross-market-coherence angle is the best remaining shot. Prompt below is current — hold the E13.13 mirage discipline (game-level collapse + PBO/DSR/FDR + the F5↔main control MUST return "consistent"). Run on the 2023→~Apr-2026 historical window now; recent-2026 completeness lands as W11/E11.20 finishes.
🎯 **THE NEW MECHANISM (why this is different from every prior null):** E5.4/E13.13/E13.8 all asked "is OUR prediction better than ONE line?" → efficient, PBO≈0.5 (our disagreement = noise). This asks a DIFFERENT question: **"are the BOOKS' OWN markets on a game mutually COHERENT, and where they CONTRADICT each other, which side does the SHARP market imply?"** An edge here does NOT require beating an efficient market on average — it requires the LAZY markets (props, team-totals, alts, F5) to be INCONSISTENT with each other / with the SHARP main line. Books price these on different desks/models at different times → internal inconsistencies are a plausible, untested inefficiency (the sharpest reading of Miller-Davidow). 🔑 the play is RELATIVE (market vs market) → partly market-NEUTRAL: we don't predict the game, we arbitrage the books' own disagreement; our model only picks WHICH side of an inconsistency to take.
SCOPE — the consistency RELATIONS to test (pre-register; cached odds + pitch-settled outcomes):
 1. ⭐ **PROPS → TEAM OFFENSE:** sum the batter prop projections (hits/TB) + implied run-scoring → does it match the **TEAM-TOTAL** line? (props + team-totals = the two LAZIEST markets → most likely inconsistent; highest prior). [needs `team_totals` in S3 — the grab below]
 2. **TEAM-TOTALS → GAME-TOTAL:** home_tt + away_tt ≈ game_total (+ vig wedge); systematic deviation = a play.
 3. **F5 → FULL-GAME = the NEGATIVE CONTROL:** E13.13 found F5 IS correctly derived off the main line (slopes matched) → this relation is EFFICIENT → if our method flags F5-vs-main as inconsistent, the METHOD is broken. Must return "consistent."
 4. **K-props → opposing TEAM-TOTAL:** high projected starter K ⇒ suppressed opposing offense ⇒ a team-total lean.
 5. **SIDES ↔ TOTALS:** the spread/total/moneyline triangle coherence.
METHOD: per relation, compute the IMPLIED quantity from market A vs the POSTED line in market B → residual = the inconsistency; settle realized outcomes → does taking the side the SHARP/implied market favors win NET OF the bet-market's vig? **Bayesian fit (your ask):** use the POSTERIOR on the implied quantity (we have the E2.3/E5.2 distributions + EB posteriors) to bet ONLY where the inconsistency exceeds the joint uncertainty with high credence.
🔒 **HONEST BAR + THE TRAP (the E13.13 lesson, non-negotiable): collapse correlated book-quotes to ONE game-level return BEFORE any significance/DSR/PBO** (E13.13's correlated-quote inflation manufactured a +29% mirage); pre-register every relation; in-fold selection; deflate for ALL relations × thresholds (DSR/FDR); judge on forward CLV net of the bet-market's vig; the F5↔main control MUST come back "consistent." HONEST PRIOR: still guarded (books link-price + sharps arb fast) — BUT a genuinely different mechanism with real value-of-information; the LAZY↔LAZY pairs (props↔team-total) are the least-arbed.
💾 DATA (§0.5): cached S3 odds + pitch-settled outcomes; NO Snowflake; one read→parquet. ✅ **DATA STATE (per the 2026-06-30 S3 audit): `team_totals`+`alternate_totals` ARE available** (derivative store `stg_derivative_odds`/`mart_derivative_closes`, →06-28; NOT the `mlb/props/` prefix → you may need to reshape/join them in). So: **relation 2 (team-total↔game-total) RUNS NOW; relation 3 (F5 control) + a weak relation 1 (existing hits/TB props → implied offense ↔ team-total) RUN NOW; relation 5 (sides↔totals) runs NOW on 2023–25** (full-game `spreads` stalled 2025-08-11 → 2026 needs the catch-up grab). The STRONG relation 1 input `batter_runs_scored`+`batter_rbis` is ✅ **NOW BACKFILLED (E5.1b, all 4 seasons) → relation 1 is RUNNABLE on the full history.** ⚠️ COORDINATION w/ W11: the derivative store (`team_totals`/`mart_derivative_closes`) is stale to ~Apr-1 until W11 wires `--w3pre` into the daily op → run E13.14 on the **2023→~Apr-2026 window NOW** (offline backtest, parallel-safe — E13.14 only READS, never edits the store W11 is fixing); the recent-2026 team-total completeness lands when W11 does. ⇒ start now on the historical window; W11 just extends the recent edge.

(Orig prompt ↓.)
🎯 THE HYPOTHESIS (operator, from finance): treat each game's odds line from first-posted → first-pitch as a PRICE TIME-SERIES (like a stock). The CLOSING line is efficient (E13.8) — but the line's TRAJECTORY may not be: the OPEN may be soft, and the line MOVING toward close is the exploitable phenomenon (steam, sharp→soft convergence, over-reaction → mean-reversion). **This is a DIFFERENT MECHANISM than everything tested** (H2H/totals/props/derivatives/cross-market all asked "is the PRICE right"; this asks "does the price's own MOVEMENT reveal structure") — and it's where real sports edges live (CLV = beating the close = the gold-standard skill measure). The program's MOST plausible remaining edge.
⚠️ **ALREADY KNOWN (don't re-run):** "follow Pinnacle/the sharp book" was tested (12.10′) → MARGINAL/no-edge (+0.0095 vs the 0.01 gate). So the naive steam-follow is ~tapped; the edge (if any) is in SUBTLER microstructure — reversion after over-moves, the open-vs-close gap on specific market/book segments, volatility regimes.
⚠️ **DATA CONSTRAINT (the honest gating fact):** microstructure needs FINE intra-window snapshots. We capture odds ~every 30 min (`odds_capture`) → GOOD granularity GOING FORWARD; HISTORICALLY coarser (open + sparse snaps + close). ⇒ the HISTORICAL backtest is suggestive only; the CLEAN honest test is PROSPECTIVE forward-CLV on the 30-min captures accruing NOW (the capture infra already exists → start accruing immediately). Frame as a forward-accruing study, not a pure backtest.
DO: (1) assemble per-game line TRAJECTORIES (open→close, all snaps, per book + consensus + sharp anchor) from the captured odds → quantify movement features: total drift, velocity, #reversals, open-close gap, sharp-soft spread over time, volatility. (2) PRE-REGISTER + test the microstructure hypotheses: does an over-move REVERT? is the OPEN beatable vs close on a market/book segment? does a signal predict the DIRECTION of the remaining move (→ bet now, capture CLV)? ⭐ **WEATHER→LINE relation (operator 2026-06-30, the most mechanistically-grounded): align the HOURLY weather time-series (W11-C's new all-slate-park capture) to the TOTAL line trajectory → does a weather change (wind shift/temp/precip-prob) PRECEDE a total move, and is there a LAG (does the book update slowly → bet the total before it reacts)?** Weather is a concrete, public, exogenous totals driver (wind at hitter parks esp.) — if the book has ANY latency updating totals on a weather change, it's exploitable. HONEST: books watch weather closely (sharp totals bettors live on wind) → the market may be efficient, but the LAG question is untested + the aligned weather+line series is new. Needs W11-C's hourly capture (its data precursor — accrues forward). ⭐ **PUBLIC-%→LINE relation (operator 2026-06-30): align the HOURLY ActionNetwork public ticket/money % (W11-D's new capture) to the line trajectory → does the line move AGAINST the public % (REVERSE LINE MOVEMENT = the classic sharp-money tell)? and does public-% divergence predict the remaining move?** HONEST: the naive "fade the public" main-line version is ~efficient (E13.8), but the aligned public-%-vs-line TIMING series (reverse-line-movement detection) is untested here. Needs W11-D's hourly capture (data precursor — accrues forward). (3) gate = FORWARD CLV net of vig (did betting at the signaled moment beat the close), deflated (PBO/DSR/FDR) across every signal × segment × threshold — the line-tick surface is a HUGE multiple-comparison space → game-level collapse + deflation MANDATORY (the E13.13/E13.14 mirage lesson).
🔒 HONEST FRAME: the historical backtest is granularity-limited/suggestive; the REAL verdict is prospective forward-CLV (capture is live → accrue ≥N games before any ship). A null is informative (the trajectory is efficient too); a survivor = a TIMING edge. Ties to E13.15 (in-game = the same line-as-series mechanism, intra-game), E2.6 (forward CLV), E13.9 (selective betting).
GATE/AC: the trajectory feature set + the pre-registered microstructure tests + the deflated result (historical-suggestive + the prospective-accrual plan) + the forward-CLV harness wired to the live captures; honest framing (granularity caveat + forward = the real test); every config logged. ⇒ a TIMING-edge candidate to confirm on forward CLV, or a trustworthy null that the line trajectory is efficient too.

▶ Story prompt — E1.12 REGIME-CONDITIONED SPECIALIZATION — do the models see too-homogeneous a slate? (market-state / mismatch-vs-market segments)   [Model · 🧭 OPUS · ⭐ operator 2026-07-04 hypothesis · CHEAPEST-FIRST bake-off under FULL deflation · a null is a valid deliverable · designed to carry into the fall college markets]   (2026-07-04; post-migration modeling-track ANCHOR — but pullable pre-ASB if a slot frees)
🟢 **READY-TO-RUN (PM 2026-07-19) — TIER-2 edge probe; its designated "post-migration ANCHOR" window is NOW (E11.1 done).** Prompt is current + already lakehouse-aware (S3/DuckDB, SF-free). Sequence it after E13.14 (fresher, market-neutral) — E1.12's mismatch-vs-market leg overlaps what E1.11/E13.8 already found (market usually right when we disagree = a feature-gap lens, not a profit segment), so set the null expectation on MLB main markets and lean into its two edge-independent payoffs (calibration-by-regime for the honest-analytics surface + the sport-agnostic harness that carries into the fall NCAAF/NCAAB thin lines). Diagnose-before-splitting; deflation counts every regime×config.
🎯 THE HYPOTHESIS (operator): our models are market-blind and predict ALL games from ONE homogeneous perspective — maybe that under-fits local structure. Would SPECIALIZING by game "regime" help? Three candidate regimes floated: (a) clear underdog (e.g. +130/-150), (b) no clear favorite / pick'em (-110/-110), (c) teams clearly mismatched by FUNDAMENTALS (W-L, Elo, Pythagorean) but the MARKET favors the lower-graded side. This is regime-conditioning / mixture-of-experts in ML terms — a legitimate way to beat a single global model that only minimizes AVERAGE loss across a heterogeneous distribution.
🧭 PM FRAMING — two DISTINCT ideas are bundled; keep them separate: **(I) market-STATE segmentation** (slice by the line's shape: underdog / pick'em) = conditioning on the market's confidence; **(II) mismatch-vs-market** (fundamentals say A, market says B) = an explicit value/contrarian signal, the only one that names a MECHANISM. Idea II is the interesting one — BUT it is essentially what `best_alpha` already tests: our model IS a fundamentals view, and comparing it to the market IS the edge search. E13.8 + E1.11 both found the market usually RIGHT when we disagree ("market favors the lower-graded team" is usually the market pricing something our features are blind to — gassed bullpen, missing bat, wind — i.e. a FEATURE-GAP detector, not a profit segment). So set expectations: on MLB MAIN markets this most-likely nulls; its real value is (i) calibration, (ii) a feature-gap lens, (iii) the TEMPLATE for the fall less-efficient college markets.
⚠️ **HONEST FRAME — market-blindness / segmentation caveat:** conditioning the model on the LINE to define a regime USES market info for segmentation → this is no longer strictly market-blind. That's fine for a SEGMENTATION study, but state it, and keep `best_alpha=0` honesty intact (no win-rate/edge claims from a lucky regime). Also: defining a regime by the line AND evaluating vs that same line is partially circular (pick'em games are ~50% base-rate BY CONSTRUCTION) → the tight target is CALIBRATION / edge-vs-the-specific-number, not raw accuracy.
🔬 **CHEAPEST-FIRST — do NOT build separate specialists first (the key technical caution):** splitting ~6 seasons into 3 regimes gives each specialist ~1/3 the data + worse variance, and separate specialists almost always LOSE to ONE well-regularized model with regime INTERACTION FEATURES unless the regimes are genuinely distinct data-generating processes. So graduate only on evidence:
 1. **DIAGNOSE first (cheap, no fragmentation):** add regime features + interactions to the EXISTING v6 substrate — a pick'em indicator, line-implied-prob, an Elo/Pythag-vs-market-disagreement flag, and their interactions with the top features. Run a **calibration-by-regime diagnostic**: does predictability / calibration ACTUALLY differ by regime (reliability curves + CRPS/logloss per regime + interaction lift)? This answers the core question without ever splitting the model.
 2. **GRADUATE only if step 1 shows genuine differential signal:** THEN run a proper §0.5 bake-off of ≥3 architectures for capturing it — (a) single model + regime interactions [the foil], (b) a gated mixture-of-experts / regime-router, (c) per-regime specialists — Optuna-tuned, feature-ablated, on the SAME purged/embargoed CV.
🔒 **DEFLATION IS NON-NEGOTIABLE (the E1.11 lesson):** regime-slicing MULTIPLIES the multiple-testing burden. PRE-REGISTER the regime partition + the candidate set BEFORE any eval; count EVERY (regime × config × architecture) toward PBO<0.2 / DSR≥0.95 / FDR; game-level correlated-quote collapse. A specialist that wins in ONE regime out of several TRIED must clear the DEFLATED bar, not its own local one. A clean null (like E1.11) is a valid, informative deliverable — do NOT manufacture a mirage against the ASB clock.
💾 **DATA/COST HYGIENE (§0.5):** read training + regime-defining data (Elo/Pythag/line) from the **S3/DuckDB lakehouse** (a Snowflake pull = RED FLAG); assemble the feature+regime matrix ONCE → parquet; every candidate / ablation / Optuna trial / CV fold reads that cached parquet (never re-read per candidate). State the S3 source + parquet path in the handoff.
🎁 **TWO PAYOFFS THAT DON'T NEED AN EDGE (bank these even on a null):** (i) **calibration-by-regime** — better-calibrated probabilities in a regime are a defensible PRODUCT improvement for the honest-analytics surface (ties E9.26) without beating anyone; (ii) **the framework is the fall multi-sport on-ramp** — "find the least-efficiently-priced segment and specialize" is a LONG shot on liquid MLB main markets but the THESIS for thin NCAAF/NCAAB lines → design the harness sport-agnostic so it re-points at college markets (ties `../../multi_sport_roadmap.md`).
🖥️ **BOX vs LAPTOP:** the diagnostic + bake-off assembly/train is heavy → **assemble-matrix + Optuna are >1-min → operator-run** (state laptop-vs-box + full copy-pasteable commands per the run-command convention); CI (fast pytest + `dbtf compile` if any dbt) on the **LAPTOP**. Lakehouse reads need `-e AWS_DEFAULT_REGION=us-east-2` if on the box.
GATE/AC: the pre-registration (regime partition + candidate set + gates, BEFORE eval); the calibration-by-regime diagnostic (per-regime reliability + interaction lift) as the graduate/stop decision; IF graduated, the deflated bake-off (≥3 architectures incl. the single-model-with-interactions foil, PBO/DSR/FDR counting every regime×config); honest framing (segmentation-uses-market caveat + `best_alpha` unchanged unless a survivor clears the deflated bar + a promotion runbook before any serve); the calibration deliverable captured for the product surface regardless; the harness left sport-agnostic for the fall. ⇒ either a regime-specialist that survives deflation (→ champion-retrain runbook), or a trustworthy null that the slate is NOT usefully heterogeneous for discrimination (with the calibration + feature-gap findings banked).

Isotonic corrects the real over-lean, keeps a non-degenerate spread, halves-plus the ECE to moneyline parity. ⚠️ **ONE SHIP-CONDITION for Part B (the nuance the session named — isotonic sits right AT the discrimination floor + totals has ~0 discrimination to protect):** the Part-B **box re-measure of served ECE is a HARD gate — if the live slate does NOT reproduce the OOF ECE improvement, do NOT ship** (it'd mean the isotonic map didn't generalize). ▶ Story prompt — E10.2 Uncertainty-aware (posterior) bet sizing   [Model/serving · staking-layer correctness · closed-form NOT RL · gated on a PROVEN edge]   (2026-06-24, synthesis)
WHY: standard fractional Kelly assumes the edge is a point estimate. Our Bayesian models produce a POSTERIOR over edge → Kelly on the posterior MEAN systematically OVERBETS because it ignores the variance in the edge estimate itself (the same Jensen's-inequality error that helped kill the totals model). We already SHOW the credible interval on every pick — we should SIZE by it too (on-brand: honest uncertainty → honest stake).
DO (closed-form, NOT RL): stake by integrating expected log-growth over the edge POSTERIOR (or the simpler equivalent: fractional Kelly shrunk by the posterior-CI width) so a wide-CI edge is staked smaller than a tight-CI edge of the same mean. + a cheap CORRELATION DISCOUNT for simultaneous bets sharing systematic risk (same pitching staff / weather / park) so correlated losses don't compound drawdown. Explicitly NOT the RL framing — over-engineering for the core win (revisit RL portfolio optimization only if multi-game effects ever become material; filed, not built).
🔒 GATE/SEQUENCING: this only matters once there's a PROVEN edge to size (E5.2 K props or an E13.13 derivative clearing the CLV gate). Don't build speculatively before an edge exists — but it's the correct sizing layer the moment one does. Cheap. HONEST: it's bet-SIZING correctness (protects the bankroll from the overbet), NOT an edge source.
```
```
▶ 🗂️ FILED SYNTHESIS IDEAS (2026-06-24) — right-tool-wrong-time / hygiene; NOT scoped as stories (revisit if conditions change):
- Kalman filter for time-varying team strength → a lighter closed-form alternative to the Sequential Prior Update Engine; a COMPUTE/COST optimization for the SPUE if its update lag ever bites. File, don't build.
- Multi-armed bandits (Thompson Sampling) for market allocation → the Bayesian-natural way to allocate attention ACROSS markets — but only once we have ≥2 PROVEN markets (K props + a derivative). Zero proven markets today. Revisit then.
- Causal inference / DAGs / do-calculus for feature validation → our leak-clean + purged-CV + orthogonality discipline already catches the worst confounding (the de-leak was a causal-validity catch). Full machinery = over-engineering for the marginal gain. Low-pri hygiene.
- Line-movement TIMING (bet-now-vs-wait) → needs tick-level odds we don't have (paid; not after a credit crunch). Defer.
- Calibration methodology (ECE/reliability/isotonic) → NOT a gap — it's a core STRENGTH (E13.6, the v6 recalibration, E13.2 ECE 0.0026); already a standing pre-deploy gate. Just apply it to the K model.
Gate/AC: explicit Phase-1 kill/proceed verdict; Phase-2 promote accuracy-first only; viz shipped; NOT in the pre-lineup path.
```

EB-shrink thin cells; emit a per-player **MLB-equivalent line + posterior uncertainty**.

▶ Story prompt — E9.30 (REDESIGN) Public "About Us" page — EDITORIAL / principles-led   [App · pure frontend · P2 · marketing/trust]   (v1 shipped 2026-06-24 → REDESIGN approved 2026-06-25)
🔁 REDESIGN — v1 shipped but the operator rejected it. v1 problems: (1) a long PROSE WALL (manifesto-length, repetitive — "honesty/uncertainty/show-our-work" ~10×); (2) it OPENED on Penumbra Partners + the penumbra philosophy; (3) zero visual design (flat white text + bold headers). And the fix is NOT to re-skin the product (a pick-card mockup just duplicated the home page). **Approved direction = EDITORIAL, principles-led, NO product UI.**
APP TARGET: UI→frontend/ ONLY — `frontend/app/about/page.tsx` (EXISTS from v1 — rewrite it). Reuse `@/components/nav` `Nav` + the static-page footer; ⛔ never legacy Streamlit. `cat frontend/package.json` first.
STRUCTURE (the approved layout — keep it tight, ~70% less copy than v1):
  1. Small eyebrow ("Credence Sports").
  2. **POV HERO** — a belief STATEMENT (not a product description), large type, e.g. "An honest maybe beats a confident guess." + a one-line subhead ("We forecast baseball the way the evidence supports — with the uncertainty shown, not hidden").
  3. **Short ORIGIN moment** — 2–3 sentences, editorial (a `font-serif` pull-treatment with a left rule reads well): the frustration that the gap between what the data can tell you and what most models admit they don't know is too wide; baseball has the most open data of any sport; the missing piece was the discipline to use it honestly.
  4. **"What we believe" — a NUMBERED PRINCIPLES LIST (4 items)**, each = a bold principle + one line (this is the load-bearing visual element — rules between rows, tabular-num indices). Suggested:
     • Show the uncertainty — every estimate carries its range; a wide one is information, not a flaw.
     • Close what fails — when a model doesn't clear its own gates, we retire it, in public, with the post-mortem.
     • **⚠️ #3 — NO FALSE CERTAINTY (worded carefully): we surface a featured pick of the day, BUT never dressed up as a sure thing — it always carries its conviction + credible interval; we don't sell win-rate streaks or guaranteed winners.** (DO NOT say "no lock of the day" / "no daily pick" — the home page HAS a featured pick; the distinction is FRAMING, not the feature.)
     • Show the work — the estimate, the range, the signals behind it, and the criteria it had to clear.
  5. **"Who it's for"** — ONE sharp sentence (the FanGraphs/Moneyball reader). ⚠️ Contrast the MINDSET ("not the person who just wants a sure thing and a good story"), NOT the feature — do NOT imply we lack a featured pick.
  6. Footer: a SINGLE "A product of Penumbra Partners" line + a CTA (e.g. "How a pick works" / sign-up).
COPY GUARDRAILS: trim hard (reader-first, not a manifesto); Penumbra = the ONE footer line ONLY (do not open on it, not a section); CUT the "Why 'Credence'" etymology + the Bayesian-epistemology aside (or compress to a single line); no repetition. 🔒 HONEST FRAMING (the brand): no edge/win-rate/beat-the-market claims (`best_alpha=0`); don't invent team/company facts.
VISUAL: editorial design — NOT product widgets (no pick cards / bars — that duplicates the home page) and NOT a flat text wall. Best spot = the **Book Comparison section of the pick-details page** (it already shows every book's line). Lower hold = a sharper, better-value book to take the price at — a natural companion to E9.11's line-shopping. Pinnacle is typically the lowest hold, reinforcing its sharp-anchor treatment.
🔗 SYNERGY / SEQUENCING: **E9.11 (best price across books) is on this EXACT surface and already computes per-book de-vig** — the hold is a byproduct of the same math (`raw_side_a + raw_side_b − 1`). If E9.11 is still in flight, STRONGLY consider folding this in there (one pass on the surface); else this is a clean fast-follow.
Read: master A0.4.32 (the per-book comparison payload — it already carries the RAW vigged implied probs per book/market, the de-vig inputs) + the Book Comparison component + `betting_ml/utils` devig_* (reuse; no new odds math) + E9.11 (same surface).
Do: compute the two-way HOLD per book per market — h2h = `raw_home_implied + raw_away_implied − 1`; totals = `raw_over_implied + raw_under_implied − 1` (the raw vigged implieds are already in the A0.4.32 payload → mostly DISPLAY math, no new data source). Show the hold % in each Book Comparison row; **highlight the LOWEST-hold (tightest) book**; optional market-consensus hold. Compute CLIENT-SIDE from the raw implieds already in the payload if present (no serving change); only add a precomputed serving field if the raw implieds aren't exposed.
**HONEST FRAMING: hold is a market-structure FACT (the book's margin), not a bet rec** — frame as "tighter book = better price to shop," consistent with the E9.11 line-shopping framing. No +EV claim.
Gate/AC: per-book hold % on Book Comparison; lowest-hold book highlighted; honest framing; reads the existing (E9.27-guarded pre-start) odds; no new odds source. **changelog entry (user-facing).**

(This expansion is REQUIRED for honesty: without netting out deposits/withdrawals, a deposit reads as "growth" — misleading. So per-book cash-flow tracking is the only way the growth % is truthful.)
DEP: E9.10 shipped `/users/profile` + the editable `initial_deposit` (DynamoDB users) — that single field GENERALIZES here (migrate it as the seed deposit on a default book). Cross-ref E9.16 Bet Log.
⚠️ COEXIST WITH P2 (INC-16): the `credence-prod-dynamo-users` table now ALSO holds a `portfolio` map (P2 moved portfolios PG→DynamoDB onto the user record) and the backend reads it via `app/backend/services/dynamo.py`. Add the bankroll fields ALONGSIDE `portfolio` — do NOT overwrite the user item / clobber that attribute (use attribute-level updates, not a full `put_item` that drops other fields). The Lambda already has this table's grant. NOTE: this is a backend/Lambda change — decoupled from the INC-16 EC2 box (orchestration), so it's safe to ship during the soak; just keep its commit separate from any INC-16 work.
Read: §5F E9.17 + §0.2 + E9.10 (the existing profile field + `/users/profile` endpoint + `services/dynamo.py`) + the Performance page (where growth shows) + the curated book set (BetMGM/Caesars/FanDuel/DraftKings/Fanatics/Bovada/Pinnacle — reuse the same names as Book Comparison).
DO:
 • DATA MODEL (DynamoDB): per-user, a set of BOOK ACCOUNTS — `{book, current_balance}` (user-editable) — plus a BANKROLL-EVENT log — `[{book, type: deposit|withdrawal, amount, date}]` (a `bankroll_events` list on the user record, or a small `credence-prod-user-bankroll-events` table keyed by Cognito `sub`). Migrate the legacy `initial_deposit` → a seed `deposit` event on a default/"unspecified" book.
 • BACKEND: extend `/users/profile` or add `/users/bankroll` endpoints — GET (books + balances + events + computed growth), PUT (edit a book's current balance; add/rename/remove a book), POST (record a deposit or withdrawal event {book, type, amount, date}). Validate amounts ≥ 0; idempotent-safe.
 • THE HONEST GROWTH MATH (the crux): per book AND overall — `net_deposits = Σ deposits − Σ withdrawals`; **betting P&L = current_balance − net_deposits**; **growth % = betting P&L / Σ deposits** (cost basis). **A deposit is NOT growth; a withdrawal is NOT a loss** — both are cash transfers netted out so the % reflects betting performance. **On the "withdrawal resets tracking" intuition: by default it does NOT reset — it's netted into the cash-flow baseline so the metric stays honest.** Offer an explicit, opt-in "reset baseline" action per book if the user truly wants a fresh start (clearly labeled; not the default).
 • FRONTEND: Settings → "Sportsbooks" — list each book with its editable current balance + an "Add deposit / Record withdrawal" control (amount + date) + an event history; "Add a sportsbook" to track more than one. Performance → OVERALL growth % + net P&L + net deposits, and a per-book breakdown; keep it LABELED DISTINCTLY from ROI (ROI = return on stake/turnover; growth = return on deposited bankroll — do NOT relabel ROI). Hide growth until at least one book + deposit is set.
 • This is a MANUAL bookkeeping ledger (user-entered balances/cash-flows) — do NOT try to auto-derive balances from settled bets (that's a different, larger feature; the Bet Log E9.16 is separate). Self-reported.
HONEST FRAMING: it's the USER's own tracked bankroll across their books — not a model edge claim; the growth % nets out cash flows so it's an honest betting-results figure, not inflated by deposits.
Gate/AC: per-book editable balances; deposit + withdrawal events recorded with date; overall + per-book growth % that NETS OUT deposits/withdrawals (a deposit doesn't inflate it, a withdrawal doesn't read as a loss); distinct from ROI; multi-book aggregation correct; legacy `initial_deposit` migrated; growth hidden until set; honest framing. `uv run pytest` green (backend calc tests). **changelog entry (user-facing).**
⚠️ SIZE: this is materially bigger than the original card (data model + endpoints + two UI surfaces) — if a session finds it too large for one pass, PHASE it: Phase 1 = the data model + per-book balance/deposit/withdrawal + the honest overall growth; Phase 2 = per-book breakdown UI + the opt-in reset. Flag the split in the handoff.
Closeout (per §0.1): END with an ⏭️ Operator handoff — run-order (DynamoDB schema/migration + lambda deploy + the `initial_deposit` migration step), `git add <paths>`, the changelog line, verify-after-deploy (add 2 books, record a deposit + a withdrawal, confirm growth % nets them out correctly).
```

```
▶ E10.1   ✅ **SHIPPED 2026-07-13 — the honest parlay CALCULATOR (build-your-own → true combined prob vs book-implied + EV + "most parlays are −EV after vig" verdict).** Ran off-box parallel to E11.20 (clean). Backend `app/backend/services/parlay_calc.py` (PURE-STDLIB — Gaussian copula for same-game correlation, Genz `bvnu` bivariate-normal, Acklam inverse-normal, EV) + `routers/parlay.py` (`GET /parlay/legs`, `POST /parlay/evaluate`) + `models/parlay.py`; frontend `app/parlay/page.tsx` + nav. Per-leg probs via the **serving cache** (E9.40 discipline → insulated from E11.20); same-game correlation-adjusted (conservative documented fallback when unavailable). ✅ **honest CALCULATOR, not the recommender** (E10.3 stays HARD-gated; no +EV/"recommend" surfacing; banned-scan green; `best_alpha=0` holds). Enhancements: book selector + auto-populated per-book lines (incl. pitcher-K props) + model-vs-book % per leg. FIXES: CORS-500 (router imported scipy → the dep-light Lambda has no numpy/scipy → ImportError at boot → made math pure-stdlib); bivariate-normal correctness (Genz `bvnu`, err 5.6e-17); matchup-TBD header fallback; `deploy.sh` S3-multipart retry hardening. Tests `test_parlay_serving.py` (22 incl. honest scan). CI 1300✅. ⏭️ E10.5 (fuller parlay surface) can follow; E10.3 recommender stays gated. (Orig prompt ↓.)
▶ Story prompt — E10.1 Parlay decision-support calculator (honest MVP)   [Model + App]
✅ **READY-STAMP (2026-07-08) — a strong on-brand parallel to E11.20/E9.43/E9.26.** 🔒 **THIS IS THE CALCULATOR, NOT THE RECOMMENDER:** show the user the TRUTH about a parlay they build (true combined prob vs book-implied + EV + an honest "most parlays are −EV after vig" verdict) — do NOT surface/"recommend" +EV parlays (that's E10.3, HARD-gated behind a proven edge we do NOT have; `best_alpha=0` holds). Honest-framing banned-language scan applies (no +EV/value/edge language; the −EV verdict is the point). ⭐ **PARALLEL-SAFETY (surface-disjoint from the 3 active sessions) — hold ALL of these:** (1) build it on its OWN parlay page/route — NOT pick-detail (E9.43's surface) and NOT the performance page (E9.26's); (2) read per-leg model probs via the **SERVING CACHE (DynamoDB→S3), NOT a direct `daily_model_predictions`/mart/lakehouse query** (the E9.40 discipline — those marts may be mid-Delta-migration under E11.20); dedup-to-latest per game (the E11.22 concern, already satisfied by `write_serving_store` on the cached blob); (3) same-game correlation = use an EXISTING/derived source (Epic 22.1 pairwise), source-stamped — do NOT build a NEW correlation pipeline over the lakehouse/box mid-E11.20; (4) OFF-BOX — frontend (Vercel) + a stateless backend calc endpoint (`app/backend/`), no serving-store-write/dbt/box. 🚨 APP-TARGET GUARD: UI=`frontend/` only; backend=`app/backend/` only; ⛔ never legacy Streamlit; `cat frontend/package.json` first. Changelog (user-facing). E10.5 (the fuller frontend parlay surface) can follow.
Read: §5G E10.1 + §0 + master Epic 22.1 (pairwise correlation) + the E9.40 scorecard (`services/scorecard.py`) for the serving-cache read + win-semantics pattern to reuse + `test_k_projection_serving.py` (the honest banned-language scan to extend).
🎯 WHAT: a build-your-own-parlay CALCULATOR that tells the user the TRUTH about the parlay they assemble — true combined probability (model) vs the book's implied probability (parlay price) + EV + a plain-language verdict — with same-game legs correlation-adjusted, not naively multiplied. Education/transparency, not a bet rec.
DO:
 0. **LEG UNIVERSE (Task 0 — sizes it):** which served markets can be legs? Start with the markets that already carry a MODEL probability in the serving cache — moneyline (`model_prob` / h2h), total_runs (over/under), and K-props (E5.5 pitcher strikeouts) if a per-leg prob is available. Cross-market legs allowed. Confirm each leg type exposes a model prob + a book price via the serving cache.
 1. **PER-LEG:** for each leg pull the **model probability** (via the SERVING CACHE — the E9.40 discipline, dedup-to-latest per game; NOT a direct mart/lakehouse query) + the **book price** (the odds the user is taking). Convert book odds → book-implied prob (de-vig per-leg where sensible, but the parlay-level implied comes from the parlay PRICE — see #3).
 2. **TRUE COMBINED PROBABILITY:** for legs in DIFFERENT games (independent) = product of per-leg model probs. For **SAME-GAME legs = correlation-ADJUSTED, never the naive product** (naive independence OVERSTATES same-game parlay prob = dishonest in the user's favor — the exact thing this tool exists to prevent). Use an EXISTING/derived pairwise-correlation source (Epic 22.1), **source-stamped**; if no correlation is available for a same-game pair, FLAG it + use a documented conservative adjustment — do NOT silently assume independence.
 3. **BOOK-IMPLIED + EV:** cross-game parlay price = product of per-leg decimal odds (computable). Same-game/SGP → the book prices it with its OWN correlation model, so the honest MVP takes the **user-entered book parlay odds** as the price (we can't infer the SGP price — that's E10.2's feasibility spike; note it). implied = 1/decimal_parlay_odds; **EV per $1 = true_prob × decimal_parlay_odds − 1**.
 4. **VERDICT (plain language, honest):** e.g. "The book's price implies {implied}%; the model estimates {true}%. Expected value ≈ {EV}% per $1 — this parlay is −EV" (or the rare ≥0 case shown factually, NOT as a "+EV play" — no recommend language). Always state that most parlays are −EV after vig.
 5. **UI (own parlay page/route — NOT pick-detail/performance):** add/remove legs (pick game → market → side; pull or enter the odds), live combined true-vs-implied + EV + verdict as legs change; a same-game-correlation-applied badge; edge-case handling (a leg with no served model prob → flag/exclude, don't fabricate).
🚨 APP-TARGET GUARD: UI=`frontend/` only (`cat frontend/package.json` first); backend=`app/backend/` (a STATELESS calc endpoint reading the serving cache — no serving-store-write/dbt/box); ⛔ never legacy Streamlit. 🔒 honest-framing banned-language scan EXTENDED to the new parlay components + green; `best_alpha=0`/`is_bet_recommendation=False` intact; NO "+EV parlay"/value/edge framing (E10.3 territory, hard-gated). Changelog (user-facing).
GATE/AC: for any user-built parlay — returns true combined prob (same-game correlation-adjusted + source-stamped, conservative-flagged when no source) vs book-implied + EV + an honest plain-language verdict; cross-game computed, same-game uses the user-entered book price (SGP-pricing gap noted → E10.2); serving-cache-only reads (insulated from E11.20); honest framing verified by the extended scan; a leg without a model prob is handled gracefully; changelog; CI green (unit tests on the prob/EV/correlation math + the honest scan). Closeout: ⏭️ operator handoff + `git add` + changelog. E10.5 (fuller parlay surface) + E10.2 (SGP-price feasibility) can follow.
```

🔢 STEP 0 — ATTRIBUTION IS IN (operator CSV, June, 5,673 credits): **lineup_monitor 30.7% · daily_ingestion 21.3% · intraday_schedule 16.0% · odds_snapshot 14.3% · statcast_catchup 7.0% · intraday_weather 5.4% · odds_current_rebuild 3.0% · pregame_snapshot 1.7% · rest <1%.** ⚠️ CORRECTS the "~95% serving chains" estimate — the two serving chains are only ~38%; the cost is SPREAD across the daily run + the capture/odds jobs.

(Same check for any of the small dormant jobs.)

▶ Story prompt — INC-14 Duplicate `is_current` lineup rows → inflated training-sample weight (investigate + fix)   [Model-A / data-correctness · 🔴 OPEN]   (surfaced by E11.1-W1d, 2026-06-25)
WHY: the W1d session downgraded a `unique_combination_of_columns(game_pk, side)` test on `feature_pregame_lineup_features` (error→warn) to unblock a merge — and it's WARNING, i.e. there ARE duplicate `(game_pk, home_away)` rows. Root-cause hypothesis: `feature_pregame_lineup_state` (SCD-2) has MULTIPLE `is_current=true` rows for the same game+side (the transition failed to flip old rows to `is_current=false`), and `feature_pregame_lineup_features.sql`'s `lineups` CTE (`WHERE is_current=true`) fans them through → the feature store → **inflated sample weight on affected games in the v6 / E2.x / E5.x training matrices.** The guard is now SOFT so this won't self-surface again. Data-correctness, not a serving outage — but it silently biases training.
DO — PHASE 1 (QUANTIFY first, don't fix blind):
 • Run the diagnostic (Snowflake MCP, read-only): `SELECT game_pk, home_away, COUNT(*) cnt FROM feature_pregame_lineup_state WHERE is_current=true GROUP BY 1,2 HAVING COUNT(*)>1 ORDER BY cnt DESC;` → HOW MANY (game×side) keys are duplicated, over WHAT date range (is it recent / all-history / a specific window?), and the dup multiplicity.
 • Trace REACH: do the dupes actually land in `feature_pregame_lineup_features` (and downstream `feature_pregame_game_features` / the training matrix)? Quantify the % of games affected in the train window → that's the inflated-weight magnitude. If it's a handful of games → minor; if systematic → assess whether v6/E2.x/E5.x need a re-fit on de-duped data.
DO — PHASE 2 (FIX the SCD-2 transition, root cause not band-aid):
 • Find where `feature_pregame_lineup_state` is written/updated (the lineup ingest / SCD-2 logic) → ensure EXACTLY ONE `is_current=true` per (game_pk, home_away): the new-lineup write must ATOMICALLY flip the prior current row(s) to `is_current=false` (or use `QUALIFY ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY game_pk, home_away ORDER BY <effective_ts> DESC)=1` to pick the latest). Add a guard so a future race can't reintroduce dupes.
 • Stopgap if the root-cause fix is involved: dedup in the `lineups` CTE (latest-effective per game×side) so the feature store is clean immediately, then fix the source.
 • RE-PROMOTE the `unique_combination_of_columns(game_pk, side)` test back to `severity: error` once clean (it's a real serving-adjacent correctness guard, not peripheral DQ — the warn downgrade was a temporary unblock).
Gate/AC: dup count quantified + training-reach assessed (with a re-fit recommendation if systematic); SCD-2 transition fixed so exactly one current row per game×side; feature store de-duped; the test back to `error` and PASSING; `uv run pytest -m "not slow"` + `dbtf compile` green. ⚠️ Snowflake reads via MCP, read-only; the long re-derive → operator.
Closeout (per §0.1): operator handoff — the diagnostic result + magnitude, the SCD-2 fix + `git add`, the test re-promotion, and the model-re-fit recommendation (if any).

▶ Story prompt — E11.16 dbt-Build CI deferral env — stop the `state:modified+` false-failures (the INC-15-class root)   [Infra · CI/CD · 🧭 OPUS · Medium]   (2026-06-25, operator — bundle into W2)
WHY: the `dbt-Build CI` runs `state:modified+` but has **NO prod deferral environment** (404 for project 441385) → partial builds hit missing-UPSTREAM nulls = **FALSE failures** (this was the `has_odds` artifact root + the noise that MASKED tonight's real W1d type break). With a deferral env, `modified+` builds resolve unbuilt upstreams from the PROD manifest instead of building/erroring on them. **AND it's compile-only today** — which is exactly how a runtime type error (the INC-15 W1d break) merged clean. Fix both.
Read: `.github/workflows/dbt_build_ci.yml` + dbt `--defer`/`--state`/`--favor-state` docs + the E11.2-T2 state pattern (`/tmp/dbt-state/`, the prod manifest already uploaded to S3 for `source_status:fresher+`) + the `has_odds` artifact (`feature_pregame_game_features_raw.sql:350`) + CLAUDE.md CI-gates.
DO:
 • Stand up a PROD deferral target: maintain/refresh the prod `manifest.json` (reuse the E11.2-T2 S3 state location) on each prod build, and add `--defer --state <prod-manifest>` (+ `--favor-state` where appropriate) to the CI `state:modified+` build → unbuilt upstreams resolve from PROD, not a partial CI build. No more missing-upstream-null false failures.
 • **RUNTIME, not compile (the INC-15 fix): the dbt-Build CI must actually RUN `dbtf build --select state:modified+` (with deferral), not just `dbtf compile`** — so a compile-clean / runtime-broken change FAILS CI before merge.
Gate/AC: CI runs `state:modified+` with a working prod deferral env (no missing-upstream-null false failures) AND actually BUILDS (runtime, not compile) → verified on a known-good change + a deliberately type-broken one (must FAIL); CI green on a clean change.
Closeout (per §0.1): operator handoff — CI workflow + state-management changes + `git add`; note the deferral-env setup steps.

Build a per-sport team-name normalization / CROSSWALK so outcomes join to the odds events (on date + normalized teams; mind doubleheaders/neutral-site). 🗒️ SESSION NOTE (2026-06-24): Scores ingestion COMPLETE — all 3 sports, all 6 seasons (2020–2025) in S3. NFL ~78% join coverage (NFL team names mostly match). NCAAF ~85% join coverage (solid). NCAAB ~27% join coverage (broken) — root cause: the Odds API uses heavy abbreviations ("St" not "State", "CSU" not "Cal State", "Loyola (Chi)" not "Loyola Chicago", "UConn Huskies" not "Connecticut Huskies", etc.) which a ~40-entry static dict cannot cover across 350+ D1 teams.
🔧 DECIDED: replace the hardcoded ESPN_CROSSWALK dict with a **DuckDB/Parquet xref table** per sport (`{sport}/crosswalk/team_names.parquet`; columns: source_name, odds_api_name, match_type). Build via `build_team_crosswalk.py` that: (1) reads all distinct odds team names from `{sport}/odds/**/*.parquet`, (2) reads all distinct ESPN source names from `{sport}/scores/**/*.parquet`, (3) auto-matches with `difflib.get_close_matches()` (cutoff ~0.80), (4) writes xref Parquet + prints unmatched pairs for manual curation. Apply crosswalk at QUERY TIME (not ingest time) — scores keep raw `home_team_source`; no re-ingest needed when the xref changes.
⏰ DEFERRED to when dbt work begins on multi-sport data (post MLB All-Star break, ~mid-July 2026). When starting that session: build `scripts/build_team_crosswalk.py` FIRST, generate and curate the xref, re-run `--validate` on all 3 scripts to confirm coverage improves before writing any dbt models.

  • ⭐ `CREATE TABLE AS SELECT … feature_pregame…` ×1,861 (~266/day) — the #1 driver; heavy feature mart fully rebuilt on (seemingly) every intraday tick.
  • `ALTER TABLE … ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS daily_model_predictions` ×8,850 (+628 dev) — idempotent DDL on every write.
  • dead Parlay inserts `parlayapi.*` ×~3,570 — pre-6/16, self-resolving post-decommission (confirm ~0 now).

  • `CREDENCE_API_RO` app-backend SELECTs (picks/narrative ROW_NUMBER) — small, watch as users grow.
Do (ROI order):
 (A) ⭐ CUT the intraday `feature_pregame` rebuild frequency = the #1 win. Determine what triggers the ~266/day full CTAS (odds_current rebuild? lineup rebuild? each fires it?) → make it INCREMENTAL or scoped, or fire only when an upstream source is actually fresher (extend E11.2-T2 `source_status:fresher+` logic to the INTRADAY path, not just daily). Don't full-rebuild the heavy mart every tick.
 (B) STOP the `ALTER ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS` per-write — move the column migration to a one-time DDL/idempotent-once path, not the prediction-write loop.
 (C) FIX the dbt-fusion QUERY_TAG so the workload is attributable (else every future audit is blind) — get the tag onto per-model queries on the fusion path; re-run snowflake_cost_by_job.py to confirm the untagged % collapses.

▶ Story prompt — E11.9-T2 Convert `feature_pregame_game_features(_raw)` full-CTAS → incremental   [Infra · cost · ⭐ biggest remaining Snowflake lever · 🔒 ML-CORRECTNESS-CRITICAL]   (2026-06-23, E11.9 deferral)
WHY: `feature_pregame_game_features(_raw)` is a full `create or replace` of the ENTIRE history on (nearly) every intraday rebuild (~3,233×/7d; E11.9-A removed only the *redundant* 2nd rebuild). Converting to `incremental` — rebuild only the games whose inputs changed, not all history — is the single biggest remaining Snowflake cut. **BUT this mart FEEDS THE LIVE SERVING PATH (predict_today + the serving store), so a stale/incorrect incremental row = bad predictions → it was deliberately deferred from E11.9 for validation. Get the SCOPE right or don't ship.**
⚠️ THE HARD PART — the incremental scope (read this twice): a scheduled game's features CHANGE through the day as lineups confirm, weather/odds/probable-pitchers land, EB posteriors update. So "rebuild today's game_pks" is NOT enough — you must re-materialize EVERY game whose upstream inputs changed since the last run, or you serve stale features. Safe filter = re-process all games with `game_date >= current_date - N` (N covering late-confirming/retro updates, e.g. 2–3 days) UNION any game whose source rows updated since the last build (ties to E11.2-T2 `source_status` thinking). Under-scope → stale features served (silent, ML-correctness bug). Over-scope → less savings but still correct (prefer this if unsure).
Read: feature_pregame_game_features.sql + feature_pregame_game_features_raw.sql (current materialization + the as-of `< game_date` guards from E1.8) + what TRIGGERS the rebuilds (pipeline/ops intraday + lineup rebuild ops) + the freshness gate that reads `_raw` build epoch (predict_today `_FRESHNESS_STALE_HOURS`) + predict_today.py (the live read) + E12 (the tier-aware serving-parity harness — REUSE it as the gate) + dbt incremental docs (unique_key, incremental_strategy merge vs delete+insert, on_schema_change).
Do:
 (1) Pick the config: `materialized='incremental'`, `unique_key` = the mart's grain (game_pk, or game_pk+side), `incremental_strategy` = `merge` or `delete+insert`, `on_schema_change='sync_all_columns'`; the `is_incremental()` filter = the SAFE scope above (date window UNION changed-source games). Preserve every E1.8 as-of guard (`< game_date`) — incremental must NOT change point-in-time semantics.
 (2) Keep a periodic FULL-REFRESH net (weekly `--full-refresh`, like the daily build) to correct any incremental drift.
 (3) VALIDATE (the gate — operator runs the >1-min dbt builds): build incremental and build full-refresh on the SAME data over a multi-day window → **assert byte-identical per game × per column** (zero diff). Specifically prove NO STALE ROWS: take a game, change an upstream input (lineup/weather), run incremental, confirm that game's features re-materialized. Then run predict_today on both → **identical predictions** (E12 harness green, all tiers). 
 (4) Measure the rebuild-cost drop (WAREHOUSE_METERING_HISTORY COMPUTE_WH vs the 57.57 cr/7d E11.9 baseline + the rebuild query count).
Gate/AC: incremental output == full-refresh (byte-identical over the window); proven no-stale-rows on an upstream change; predict_today predictions UNCHANGED (E12 parity green, all tiers); weekly full-refresh net retained; measured credit/rebuild-count reduction; `uv run pytest` + `dbtf compile` green; changelog = none (infra, predictions must NOT change).
Closeout (per §0.1): the long `dbtf build` validations → operator; ⏭️ Operator handoff — the incremental-vs-full parity evidence + the no-stale-rows proof + the predict_today parity + the credit delta + git add. If parity is NOT perfect, DO NOT ship — revert to full-CTAS and report the diff.

```
▶ Story prompt — E13.0 home_win/pre forward-validation   ✅ DONE 2026-06-21 — HOLD-for-deploy.
Pass-2 thin/ambiguous (completed seasons −0.0030 Brier, barely over the 0.002 floor; 2026 +0.0017 ≈ wash). home_win = confirmed thin-signal target → challenger registered, deploy WITHHELD; a 3rd-decimal edge isn't worth bespoke forward infra. 🔬 VERDICT — E13.0 (2026-06-21): **an offline re-run is NOT a valid 2nd hysteresis window. DEPLOY WITHHELD; the 2nd pass must come from FORWARD live-retention, not a re-gate.** Proof (verified against gate code): `evaluate_promotion` computes the entire decision — pooled Δ, paired-bootstrap CI, and the no-season-regression check — over `comp_mask = completed_seasons {2024,2025}` ONLY; 2026 is `current_season`, corroboration-only, never in the decision. The 2024/2025 per-game scores are a deterministic function of frozen historical rows (point-in-time-as-of-game; games already played) + fixed seed=42 (glm challenger + xgb/Platt baseline both deterministic). ⇒ **Absent an upstream historical restatement, a `--refresh-cache` re-run reproduces pass-1 BYTE-FOR-BYTE on the decisive folds (2024 Δ−0.00378, 2025 Δ−0.00387) → deterministically PROMOTE again.** Two offline gates 2 days apart are NOT independent windows: they share ~99.6% of decisive data, and the program's own hysteresis design (`promotion_gate.py:32`, `MIN_CONSECUTIVE_PASSES=2`) explicitly demands "a respected re-eval interval … to stop monthly redeploys chasing early-season regime noise." Rubber-stamping deploy off a deterministic re-gate would manufacture false hysteresis. The offline verdict is in fact FROZEN at PROMOTE until 2026 itself becomes a completed season (months out). **Pass-1 evidence archived** → `gate_v6_vs_v5_home_win_pre_lineup_pass1_2026-06-19.json` (the canonical gate_json filename is variant-derived and WILL be clobbered by any re-run).

  | window | pooled Δ | CI | 2024 Δ (n) | 2025 Δ (n) | 2026 Δ (n) |
  |---|---|---|---|---|---|
  | pass-1 (06-19) | −0.0038 | [−0.0055,−0.0021] | −0.0038 (2000) | −0.0039 (2026) | +0.0012 (838) |
  | pass-2 (06-21) | −0.0030 | [−0.0047,−0.0014] | **−0.0021** (2001) | −0.0039 (2026) | **+0.0017** (864) |
  - **My "byte-identical absent restatement" prediction was FALSIFIED → the marts are NOT frozen.** Fresh pull = 10,836→10,866 rows (+26 new 2026 games, +1 2024 game, +3 training-season). The 2024 fold MOVED: edge nearly **halved** (−0.0038→−0.0021, now barely clears the 0.002 floor on 2024 alone). Mechanism: the **baseline IMPROVED** under backfill (2024 champ Brier 0.2464→0.2448) while the challenger stayed flat (0.2426→0.2427) — as the arsenal/Stuff+/bullpen backfill fills historical features in, the richer 154-feat xgb closes the gap on the lean 36-feat glm. So the "movement" is feature-restatement on the SAME games, NOT new independent observations → still NOT a clean independent hysteresis window.
  - **Every forward-leaning signal is unsupportive:** 2026 (newest, genuinely-new games, the most forward-like fold) has the challenger BEHIND in BOTH passes and the gap WIDENED (+0.0012→+0.0017). The PROMOTE rests entirely on completed 2024+2025; on the freshest OOS data the 36-feat glm is slightly worse than the served morning baseline — the "wins on completed/backfilled history, behind on fresh OOS" shape, the exact v5-collapse failure mode the WHY warns about, now faintly visible in v6 on 2026.
VERDICT STANDS: **DEPLOY WITHHELD** — now on EVIDENCE, not just methodology. Pass-2 archived → `gate_v6_vs_v5_home_win_pre_lineup_pass2_2026-06-21.json` (canonical gate_json now = pass-2). Robustness is deteriorating under restatement; the live-leaning read is negative.
WHAT TO ACTUALLY DO: the real 2nd pass = **forward/serving-parity**: shadow-serve the 36-feat glm on live morning picks and score vs the served 154-feat champion on 2026 games AS THEY COMPLETE (ties into E12, structurally PASS). Crucial nuance pass-2 exposes — the offline edge shrinks as features get BACKFILLED toward completeness, but LIVE morning serving is SPARSE/point-in-time-incomplete (the 30.3 finding), so neither model sees complete features live; which regime predicts live ranking is unknown → only forward-validation on actually-served sparse features answers it. ▶ Story prompt — E13.8 Market-accuracy benchmark: year×book line quality (H2H + totals)   [Model-A · situational awareness · advisory/transparency only]   (2026-06-23, operator)

(4) ANCHOR with REFERENCE ROWS so the numbers are interpretable: the base-rate/no-skill Brier (H2H ≈ 0.249 from home-win rate; totals ≈ 0.25 from the over rate) and an explicit "Pinnacle = ceiling" callout. ▶ Story prompt — E13.9 Selective "best-bet" model: abstention + betting-utility objective on the SOFT markets   [Model-A · ⭐ distinct edge angle · market-AWARE exception · full LdP discipline]   (2026-06-23, operator)
🟢 **READY-TO-RUN (PM 2026-07-19) — TIER-2 edge probe, but LOWERED: run AFTER E13.14.** Its soft-market target substantially overlaps E13.14 (which probes the same lazy markets — props/team-totals — more directly), so let E13.14 run first and reuse what it learns about WHERE the soft markets are inconsistent to seed E13.9's selection rule. Prompt below is current (S3/DuckDB, SF-free, revive the E13.5 shadow-serve harness for forward-CLV accrual). Still the sanctioned selective-abstention successor to the killed E3.1/E4/E13.1 hunt; likely null but doubles as an honest "biggest-disagreement picks" product surface.
WHY: every edge test so far graded the model on predicting EVERY game (minimize Brier over all games) or anchored to the line (E13.1). The operator's idea: build a model that DISCRIMINATES on the best bets — abstain on most games, fire only on a selected subset, and judge it on that subset's payoff, not all-games accuracy. This is alpha-from-SELECTION (complement to E13.4's alpha-from-features).
🔑 WHAT MAKES IT DISTINCT FROM THE KILLED E13.1 (read this first — do NOT rebuild E13.1): E13.1 trained on all games, anchored to the line, learned the residual → dead on CLV. E13.9 is different on TWO axes: (1) the OBJECTIVE is itself selective — directly optimize the SELECTED-subset payoff (expected CLV / betting utility) with an explicit ABSTENTION mechanism (the model chooses when NOT to bet), NOT "minimize all-games loss then threshold the output"; (2) it targets the SOFT markets — totals-derivatives (team totals / alt totals; data exists in mart_derivative_closes via E2.0) and player props (once E5.1 lands) — where E13.8 showed the main line is efficient (Brier ~0.250) but the lazier derivative/alt prices may not be. The MAIN H2H + main totals lines are a NEGATIVE CONTROL only (expect null per E13.8/E13.1).
⚠️ THE TRAP — this framing manufactures fake edges if done naively. "Backtest, keep the games we'd have won, call those best bets" is pure data-mining. GUARDRAILS (non-negotiable, pre-register ALL before any forward look): the selection rule + abstention threshold are PART of the model — fit IN-FOLD, validated OUT-OF-FOLD (purged/embargoed CV); the subset size is pre-committed or swept in-fold, NEVER chosen to flatter the result; the verdict is FORWARD/held-out CLV on the SELECTED subset (the cashability gate), with PBO<0.2 + DSR>0 (DSR deflates for the number of configs tried — log every config). Market-AWARE is in scope here (explicit exception, like E13.1) — judged on beating the close, not accuracy.
🔬 BAKE-OFF (per §0.5): the selective architecture is NOT one design — pre-register a CANDIDATE SET of ≥3 selection/abstention approaches and bake them off, Optuna-tuned, judged on forward/held-out CLV on the SELECTED subset under purged CV, PBO<0.2/DSR>0 (the deflation prices in the search). The "e.g." forms below are the candidate set, not a pick-one menu; a single design's miss is NOT a null.
DO: (1) bake off the selective architectures — e.g. (a) an expected-value/utility objective over (model fair prob/total vs the book's de-vigged price) with an abstain action, (b) a two-stage "is THIS a bettable edge?" gate trained to predict realized CLV-positivity, (c) a conformal/selective-prediction wrapper over the calibrated model with a tuned abstention threshold — each candidate market vs its OWN close (per the E2.6 derivative-gate pattern), each Optuna-tuned, the subset size swept in-fold; (2) run them on totals-derivatives FIRST (E2.0 data ready), props later (post-E5.1); (3) main lines as the negative control; (4) the long CV/forward fits go to the operator. Stratify on is_cold_start (E13.7) where pitcher inputs matter.
MEASUREMENT: this is the consumer that REVIVES E13.5 (generic shadow-serve + forward-CLV harness) — stand up E13.5 to shadow-serve the selective policy and accrue forward CLV on the selected subset as games complete. Offline backtest CLV is necessary-not-sufficient; the real verdict is forward.
HONEST EXPECTATION: likely NULL — market efficiency is confirmed from E3.1/E4/E1.9/E13.1/E13.8. But it's a genuinely distinct angle and a clean leak-tight null completes the dossier; a soft-market subset hit would be the program's FIRST real betting edge. PRODUCT NOTE (separate from edge): even a null-edge selective layer can power a "highest-conviction / biggest-disagreement picks of the day" surface — but framed HONESTLY (higher-variance, "our model's biggest disagreements with the market," NO +EV/beat-the-book claim) unless it clears the CLV gate. Coordinate that surface with E9/honest-framing.
💾 DATA (per §0.5): `mart_derivative_closes` (E2.0) is in S3 — read via DuckDB; assemble the selection-model feature matrix in ONE pull → parquet and run every selective-architecture candidate × Optuna trial × fold off the cache, never re-query per candidate.
Read: build_roadmap E13.9 row + the E13.1 kill writeup (what NOT to repeat) + E13.8 benchmark (the soft-vs-main-line bar) + E2.6 derivative-gate spec + mart_derivative_closes (E2.0) + betting_ml eval discipline (purged CV / PBO / DSR) + E13.5 prompt (the harness to revive).
Gate/AC: pre-registered selection rule + abstention + subset size; offline selected-subset CLV with PBO<0.2/DSR>0 per market; E13.5 shadow-serve stood up for forward accrual; honest dossier entry (incl. a null). NO +EV product claim without the forward CLV gate. No changelog unless a user-facing surface ships.
Closeout (per §0.1): long fits → operator (run-order, >1-min flagged); ⏭️ handoff = the design doc + ablation_results per market + E13.5 harness + git add. SEQUENCE: after E13.4 (use its winning features) + E5.1 (props); totals-derivatives can start sooner.
